### Networking

*   [arp (‚≠ê313)](https://github.com/mdlayher/arp) - Package arp implements the ARP protocol, as described in RFC 826.
*   [buffstreams (‚≠ê254)](https://github.com/stabbycutyou/buffstreams) - Streaming protocolbuffer data over TCP made easy.
*   [canopus (‚≠ê151)](https://github.com/zubairhamed/canopus) - CoAP Client/Server implementation (RFC 7252).
*   [cidranger (‚≠ê819)](https://github.com/yl2chen/cidranger) - Fast IP to CIDR lookup for Go.
*   [dhcp6 (‚≠ê76)](https://github.com/mdlayher/dhcp6) - Package dhcp6 implements a DHCPv6 server, as described in RFC 3315.
*   [dns (‚≠ê6.9k)](https://github.com/miekg/dns) - Go library for working with DNS.
*   [dnsmonster (‚≠ê250)](https://github.com/mosajjal/dnsmonster) - Passive DNS Capture/Monitoring Framework.
*   [easytcp (‚≠ê656)](https://github.com/DarthPestilane/easytcp) - A light-weight TCP framework written in Go (Golang), built with message router. EasyTCP helps you build a TCP server easily fast and less painful.
*   [ether (‚≠ê78)](https://github.com/songgao/ether) - Cross-platform Go package for sending and receiving ethernet frames.
*   [ethernet (‚≠ê256)](https://github.com/mdlayher/ethernet) - Package ethernet implements marshaling and unmarshaling of IEEE 802.3 Ethernet II frames and IEEE 802.1Q VLAN tags.
*   [fasthttp (‚≠ê19k)](https://github.com/valyala/fasthttp) - Package fasthttp is a fast HTTP implementation for Go, up to 10 times faster than net/http.
*   [fortio (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/fortio/fortio) - Load testing library and command line tool, advanced echo server and web UI. Allows to specify a set query-per-second load and record latency histograms and other useful stats and graph them. Tcp, Http, gRPC.
*   [ftp (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/jlaffaye/ftp) - Package ftp implements a FTP client as described in [RFC 959](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc959).
*   [ftpserverlib (‚≠ê351)](https://github.com/fclairamb/ftpserverlib) - Fully featured FTP server library.
*   [gaio (‚≠ê488)](https://github.com/xtaci/gaio) - High performance async-io networking for Golang in proactor mode.
*   [gev (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/Allenxuxu/gev) - gev is a lightweight, fast non-blocking TCP network library based on Reactor mode.
*   [gmqtt (‚≠ê855)](https://github.com/DrmagicE/gmqtt) - Gmqtt is a flexible, high-performance MQTT broker library that fully implements the MQTT protocol V3.1.1.
*   [gnet (‚≠ê7.6k)](https://github.com/panjf2000/gnet) - `gnet` is a high-performance, lightweight, non-blocking, event-driven networking framework written in pure Go.
*   [gNxI (‚≠ê233)](https://github.com/google/gnxi) - A collection of tools for Network Management that use the gNMI and gNOI protocols.
*   [go-getter (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-getter) - Go library for downloading files or directories from various sources using a URL.
*   [go-powerdns (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/joeig/go-powerdns) - PowerDNS API bindings for Golang.
*   [go-stun (‚≠ê567)](https://github.com/ccding/go-stun) - Go implementation of the STUN client (RFC 3489 and RFC 5389).
*   [gobgp (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/osrg/gobgp) - BGP implemented in the Go Programming Language.
*   [golibwireshark (‚≠ê29)](https://github.com/sunwxg/golibwireshark) - Package golibwireshark use libwireshark library to decode pcap file and analyse dissection data.
*   [gopacket (‚≠ê5.6k)](https://github.com/google/gopacket) - Go library for packet processing with libpcap bindings.
*   [gopcap (‚≠ê471)](https://github.com/akrennmair/gopcap) - Go wrapper for libpcap.
*   [goshark (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/sunwxg/goshark) - Package goshark use tshark to decode IP packet and create data struct to analyse packet.
*   [gosnmp (‚≠ê952)](https://github.com/soniah/gosnmp) - Native Go library for performing SNMP actions.
*   [gotcp (‚≠ê506)](https://github.com/gansidui/gotcp) - Go package for quickly writing tcp applications.
*   [grab (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/cavaliercoder/grab) - Go package for managing file downloads.
*   [graval (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/koofr/graval) - Experimental FTP server framework.
*   [HTTPLab (‚≠ê3.9k)](https://github.com/gchaincl/httplab) - HTTPLabs let you inspect HTTP requests and forge responses.
*   [httpproxy (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/wzshiming/httpproxy) - HTTP proxy handler and dialer.
*   [iplib (‚≠ê108)](https://github.com/c-robinson/iplib) - Library for working with IP addresses (net.IP, net.IPNet), inspired by python [ipaddress](https://docs.python.org/3/library/ipaddress.html) and ruby [ipaddr](https://ruby-doc.org/stdlib-2.5.1/libdoc/ipaddr/rdoc/IPAddr.html)
*   [jazigo (‚≠ê190)](https://github.com/udhos/jazigo) - Jazigo is a tool written in Go for retrieving configuration for multiple network devices.
*   [kcp-go (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/xtaci/kcp-go) - KCP - Fast and Reliable ARQ Protocol.
*   [kcptun (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/xtaci/kcptun) - Extremely simple & fast udp tunnel based on KCP protocol.
*   [lhttp (‚≠ê683)](https://github.com/fanux/lhttp) - Powerful websocket framework, build your IM server more easily.
*   [linkio (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/ian-kent/linkio) - Network link speed simulation for Reader/Writer interfaces.
*   [llb (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/kirillDanshin/llb) - It's a very simple but quick backend for proxy servers. Can be useful for fast redirection to predefined domain with zero memory allocation and fast response.
*   [mdns (‚≠ê968)](https://github.com/hashicorp/mdns) - Simple mDNS (Multicast DNS) client/server library in Golang.
*   [mqttPaho](https://eclipse.org/paho/clients/golang/) - The Paho Go Client provides an MQTT client library for connection to MQTT brokers via TCP, TLS or WebSockets.
*   [nbio (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/lesismal/nbio) - Pure Go 1000k+ connections solution, support tls/http1.x/websocket and basically compatible with net/http, with high-performance and low memory cost, non-blocking, event-driven, easy-to-use.
*   [netpoll (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/cloudwego/netpoll) - A high-performance non-blocking I/O networking framework, which focused on RPC scenarios, developed by ByteDance.
*   [NFF-Go (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/intel-go/nff-go) - Framework for rapid development of performant network functions for cloud and bare-metal (former YANFF).
*   [packet (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/aerogo/packet) - Send packets over TCP and UDP. It can buffer messages and hot-swap connections if needed.
*   [panoptes-stream (‚≠ê39)](https://github.com/yahoo/panoptes-stream) - A cloud native distributed streaming network telemetry (gNMI, Juniper JTI and Cisco MDT).
*   [peerdiscovery (‚≠ê588)](https://github.com/schollz/peerdiscovery) - Pure Go library for cross-platform local peer discovery using UDP multicast.
*   [portproxy (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/aybabtme/portproxy) - Simple TCP proxy which adds CORS support to API's which don't support it.
*   [publicip (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/polera/publicip) - Package publicip returns your public facing IPv4 address (internet egress).
*   [quic-go (‚≠ê8.1k)](https://github.com/lucas-clemente/quic-go) - An implementation of the QUIC protocol in pure Go.
*   [raw (‚≠ê423)](https://github.com/mdlayher/raw) - Package raw enables reading and writing data at the device driver level for a network interface.
*   [sftp (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/pkg/sftp) - Package sftp implements the SSH File Transfer Protocol as described in <https://filezilla-project.org/specs/draft-ietf-secsh-filexfer-02.txt>.
*   [ssh (‚≠ê3k)](https://github.com/gliderlabs/ssh) - Higher-level API for building SSH servers (wraps crypto/ssh).
*   [sslb (‚≠ê143)](https://github.com/eduardonunesp/sslb) - It's a Super Simples Load Balancer, just a little project to achieve some kind of performance.
*   [stun (‚≠ê487)](https://github.com/go-rtc/stun) - Go implementation of RFC 5389 STUN protocol.
*   [tcp\_server (‚≠ê420)](https://github.com/firstrow/tcp_server) - Go library for building tcp servers faster.
*   [tspool (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/two/tspool) - A TCP Library use worker pool to improve performance and protect your server.
*   [utp (‚≠ê166)](https://github.com/anacrolix/utp) - Go uTP micro transport protocol implementation.
*   [vssh (‚≠ê893)](https://github.com/yahoo/vssh) - Go library for building network and server automation over SSH protocol.
*   [water (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/songgao/water) - Simple TUN/TAP library.
*   [webrtc (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/pions/webrtc) - A pure Go implementation of the WebRTC API.
*   [winrm (‚≠ê402)](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm) - Go WinRM client to remotely execute commands on Windows machines.
*   [xtcp (‚≠ê142)](https://github.com/xfxdev/xtcp) - TCP Server Framework with simultaneous full duplex communication, graceful shutdown, and custom protocol.

### HTTP Clients

*   [gentleman (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/h2non/gentleman) - Full-featured plugin-driven HTTP client library.
*   [go-http-client (‚≠ê52)](https://github.com/bozd4g/go-http-client) - Make http calls simply and easily.
*   [go-req (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/wenerme/go-req) - Declarative golang HTTP client.
*   [go-retryablehttp (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-retryablehttp) - Retryable HTTP client in Go.
*   [grequests (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/levigross/grequests) - A Go "clone" of the great and famous Requests library.
*   [heimdall (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/gojektech/heimdall) - An enhanced http client with retry and hystrix capabilities.
*   [httpretry (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/ybbus/httpretry) - Enriches the default go HTTP client with retry functionality.
*   [pester (‚≠ê615)](https://github.com/sethgrid/pester) - Go HTTP client calls with retries, backoff, and concurrency.
*   [request (‚≠ê231)](https://github.com/monaco-io/request) - HTTP client for golang. If you have experience about axios or requests, you will love it. No 3rd dependency.
*   [requests (‚≠ê578)](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/requests) - HTTP requests for Gophers. Uses context.Context and doesn't hide the underlying net/http.Client, making it compatible with standard Go APIs. Also includes testing tools.
*   [resty (‚≠ê7.6k)](https://github.com/go-resty/resty) - Simple HTTP and REST client for Go inspired by Ruby rest-client.
*   [rq (‚≠ê46)](https://github.com/ddo/rq) - A nicer interface for golang stdlib HTTP client.
*   [sling (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/dghubble/sling) - Sling is a Go HTTP client library for creating and sending API requests.

### OpenGL

*   [gl (‚≠ê959)](https://github.com/go-gl/gl) - Go bindings for OpenGL (generated via glow).
*   [glfw (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/go-gl/glfw) - Go bindings for GLFW 3.

### ORM

*   [cacheme (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/Yiling-J/cacheme-go) - Schema based, typed Redis caching/memoize framework for Go.
*   [ent (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/facebook/ent) - An entity framework for Go. Simple, yet powerful ORM for modeling and querying data.
*   [go-firestorm (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/jschoedt/go-firestorm) - A simple ORM for Google/Firebase Cloud Firestore.
*   [go-sql (‚≠ê172)](https://github.com/rushteam/gosql) - A easy ORM for mysql.
*   [go-sqlbuilder (‚≠ê975)](https://github.com/huandu/go-sqlbuilder) - A flexible and powerful SQL string builder library plus a zero-config ORM.
*   [go-store (‚≠ê110)](https://github.com/gosuri/go-store) - Simple and fast Redis backed key-value store library for Go.
*   [GORM (‚≠ê32k)](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) - The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly.
*   [gormt (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) - Mysql database to golang gorm struct.
*   [gorp (‚≠ê3.7k)](https://github.com/go-gorp/gorp) - Go Relational Persistence, ORM-ish library for Go.
*   [grimoire (‚≠ê158)](https://github.com/Fs02/grimoire) - Grimoire is a database access layer and validation for golang. (Support: MySQL, PostgreSQL and SQLite3).
*   [lore (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) - Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go.
*   [marlow (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) - Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances.
*   [pop/soda (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
*   [Prisma (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/prisma/prisma-client-go) - Prisma Client Go, Typesafe database access for Go.
*   [reform (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/go-reform/reform) - Better ORM for Go, based on non-empty interfaces and code generation.
*   [rel (‚≠ê634)](https://github.com/go-rel/rel) - Modern Database Access Layer for Golang - Testable, Extendable and Crafted Into a Clean and Elegant API.
*   [SQLBoiler (‚≠ê5.7k)](https://github.com/volatiletech/sqlboiler) - ORM generator. Generate a featureful and blazing-fast ORM tailored to your database schema.
*   [upper.io/db (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/upper/db) - Single interface for interacting with different data sources through the use of adapters that wrap mature database drivers.
*   [XORM](https://gitea.com/xorm/xorm) - Simple and powerful ORM for Go. (Support: MySQL, MyMysql, PostgreSQL, Tidb, SQLite3, MsSql and Oracle).
*   [Zoom (‚≠ê299)](https://github.com/albrow/zoom) - Blazing-fast datastore and querying engine built on Redis.

### Package Management

*   [go modules](https://golang.org/cmd/go/#hdr-Modules__module_versions__and_more) - Modules are the unit of source code interchange and versioning. The go command has direct support for working with modules, including recording and resolving dependencies on other modules.

*   [vgo](https://go.googlesource.com/vgo/) - Versioned Go.
*   [glide (‚≠ê8.2k)](https://github.com/Masterminds/glide) - Manage your golang vendor and vendored packages with ease. Inspired by tools like Maven, Bundler, and Pip.
*   [godep (‚≠ê5.6k)](https://github.com/tools/godep) - dependency tool for go, godep helps build packages reproducibly by fixing their dependencies.

*   [goop (‚≠ê779)](https://github.com/nitrous-io/goop) - Simple dependency manager for Go (golang), inspired by Bundler.
*   [gop (‚≠ê50)](https://github.com/lunny/gop) - Build and manage your Go applications out of GOPATH.
*   [gopm (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/gpmgo/gopm) - Go Package Manager.
*   [govendor (‚≠ê5k)](https://github.com/kardianos/govendor) - Go Package Manager. Go vendor tool that works with the standard vendor file.
*   [gpm (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/pote/gpm) - Barebones dependency manager for Go.
*   [johnny-deps (‚≠ê214)](https://github.com/VividCortex/johnny-deps) - Minimal dependency version using Git.
*   [modgv (‚≠ê449)](https://github.com/lucasepe/modgv) - Converts 'go mod graph' output into Graphviz's DOT language.
*   [mvn-golang (‚≠ê150)](https://github.com/raydac/mvn-golang) - plugin that provides way for auto-loading of Golang SDK, dependency management and start build environment in Maven project infrastructure.
*   [nut (‚≠ê238)](https://github.com/jingweno/nut) - Vendor Go dependencies.
*   [VenGO (‚≠ê124)](https://github.com/DamnWidget/VenGO) - create and manage exportable isolated go virtual environments.

### Resource Embedding

*   [debme (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/leaanthony/debme) - Create an `embed.FS` from an existing `embed.FS` subdirectory.

*   [go.rice (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/GeertJohan/go.rice) - go.rice is a Go package that makes working with resources such as HTML, JS, CSS, images, and templates very easy.
*   [mule (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/wlbr/mule) - Embed external resources like images, movies ... into Go source code to create single file binaries using `go generate`. Focused on simplicity.
*   [packr (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/packr) - The simple and easy way to embed static files into Go binaries.
*   [rebed (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/soypat/rebed) - Recreate folder structures and files from Go 1.16's `embed.FS` type
*   [statics (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/go-playground/statics) - Embeds static resources into go files for single binary compilation + works with http.FileSystem + symlinks.
*   [statik (‚≠ê3.6k)](https://github.com/rakyll/statik) - Embeds static files into a Go executable.
*   [templify (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/wlbr/templify) - Embed external template files into Go code to create single file binaries.
*   [vfsgen (‚≠ê967)](https://github.com/shurcooL/vfsgen) - Generates a vfsdata.go file that statically implements the given virtual filesystem.

### Science and Data Analysis

*   [assocentity (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/ndabAP/assocentity) - Package assocentity returns the average distance from words to a given entity.

*   [chart (‚≠ê753)](https://github.com/vdobler/chart) - Simple Chart Plotting library for Go. Supports many graphs types.
*   [dataframe-go (‚≠ê975)](https://github.com/rocketlaunchr/dataframe-go) - Dataframes for machine-learning and statistics (similar to pandas).
*   [decimal (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/db47h/decimal) - Package decimal implements arbitrary-precision decimal floating-point arithmetic.
*   [evaler (‚≠ê51)](https://github.com/soniah/evaler) - Simple floating point arithmetic expression evaluator.
*   [ewma (‚≠ê405)](https://github.com/VividCortex/ewma) - Exponentially-weighted moving averages.
*   [geom (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/skelterjohn/geom) - 2D geometry for golang.
*   [go-dsp (‚≠ê813)](https://github.com/mjibson/go-dsp) - Digital Signal Processing for Go.
*   [go-estimate (‚≠ê104)](https://github.com/milosgajdos/go-estimate) - State estimation and filtering algorithms in Go.
*   [go-gt (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/ThePaw/go-gt) - Graph theory algorithms written in "Go" language.
*   [godesim (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/soypat/godesim) - Extended/multivariable ODE solver framework for event-based simulations with simple API.
*   [goent (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/kzahedi/goent) - GO Implementation of Entropy Measures.
*   [gohistogram (‚≠ê171)](https://github.com/VividCortex/gohistogram) - Approximate histograms for data streams.
*   [gonum (‚≠ê6.5k)](https://github.com/gonum/gonum) - Gonum is a set of numeric libraries for the Go programming language. It contains libraries for matrices, statistics, optimization, and more.
*   [gonum/plot (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/gonum/plot) - gonum/plot provides an API for building and drawing plots in Go.
*   [goraph (‚≠ê713)](https://github.com/gyuho/goraph) - Pure Go graph theory library(data structure, algorithm visualization).
*   [gosl (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/cpmech/gosl) - Go scientific library for linear algebra, FFT, geometry, NURBS, numerical methods, probabilities, optimisation, differential equations, and more.
*   [GoStats (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/OGFris/GoStats) - GoStats is an Open Source GoLang library for math statistics mostly used in Machine Learning domains, it covers most of the Statistical measures functions.
*   [graph (‚≠ê636)](https://github.com/yourbasic/graph) - Library of basic graph algorithms.
*   [jsonl-graph (‚≠ê63)](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/jsonl-graph) - Tool to manipulate JSONL graphs with graphviz support.
*   [ode (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/ode) - Ordinary differential equation (ODE) solver which supports extended states and channel-based iteration stop conditions.
*   [orb (‚≠ê647)](https://github.com/paulmach/orb) - 2D geometry types with clipping, GeoJSON and Mapbox Vector Tile support.
*   [pagerank (‚≠ê78)](https://github.com/alixaxel/pagerank) - Weighted PageRank algorithm implemented in Go.
*   [piecewiselinear (‚≠ê24)](https://github.com/sgreben/piecewiselinear) - Tiny linear interpolation library.
*   [PiHex (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/claygod/PiHex) - Implementation of the "Bailey-Borwein-Plouffe" algorithm for the hexadecimal number Pi.
*   [rootfinding (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/khezen/rootfinding) - root-finding algorithms library for finding roots of quadratic functions.
*   [sparse (‚≠ê141)](https://github.com/james-bowman/sparse) - Go Sparse matrix formats for linear algebra supporting scientific and machine learning applications, compatible with gonum matrix libraries.
*   [stats (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/montanaflynn/stats) - Statistics package with common functions missing from the Golang standard library.
*   [streamtools (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/nytlabs/streamtools) - general purpose, graphical tool for dealing with streams of data.
*   [TextRank (‚≠ê178)](https://github.com/DavidBelicza/TextRank) - TextRank implementation in Golang with extendable features (summarization, weighting, phrase extraction) and multithreading (goroutine) support.
*   [triangolatte (‚≠ê35)](https://github.com/tchayen/triangolatte) - 2D triangulation library. Allows translating lines and polygons (both based on points) to the language of GPUs.

### Security

*   [acmetool (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.
*   [acra (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) - Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system.
*   [age (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability.
*   [argon2-hashing (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.
*   [argon2pw (‚≠ê89)](https://github.com/raja/argon2pw) - Argon2 password hash generation with constant-time password comparison.
*   [autocert](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/crypto/acme/autocert) - Auto provision Let's Encrypt certificates and start a TLS server.
*   [BadActor (‚≠ê313)](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.
*   [Cameradar (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/Ullaakut/cameradar) - Tool and library to remotely hack RTSP streams from surveillance cameras.
*   [certificates (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) - An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates.
*   [CertMagic (‚≠ê4.4k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) - Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal.
*   [dongle (‚≠ê693)](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding\&decoding and encryption\&decryption.
*   [firewalld-rest (‚≠ê330)](https://github.com/prashantgupta24/firewalld-rest) - A rest application to dynamically update firewalld rules on a linux server.
*   [go-generate-password (‚≠ê48)](https://github.com/m1/go-generate-password) - Password generator that can be used on the cli or as a library.
*   [go-htpasswd (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/tg123/go-htpasswd) - Apache htpasswd Parser for Go.
*   [go-password-validator (‚≠ê399)](https://github.com/lane-c-wagner/go-password-validator) - Password validator based on raw cryptographic entropy values.
*   [go-yara (‚≠ê292)](https://github.com/hillu/go-yara) - Go Bindings for [YARA (‚≠ê132)](https://github.com/plusvic/yara), the "pattern matching swiss knife for malware researchers (and everyone else)".
*   [goArgonPass (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/dwin/goArgonPass) - Argon2 password hash and verification designed to be compatible with existing Python and PHP implementations.
*   [goSecretBoxPassword (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/dwin/goSecretBoxPassword) - A probably paranoid package for securely hashing and encrypting passwords.
*   [Interpol](https://bitbucket.org/vahidi/interpol) - Rule-based data generator for fuzzing and penetration testing.
*   [lego (‚≠ê6k)](https://github.com/go-acme/lego) - Pure Go ACME client library and CLI tool (for use with Let's Encrypt).
*   [memguard (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/awnumar/memguard) - A pure Go library for handling sensitive values in memory.
*   [nacl (‚≠ê537)](https://github.com/kevinburke/nacl) - Go implementation of the NaCL set of API's.
*   [optimus-go (‚≠ê338)](https://github.com/pjebs/optimus-go) - ID hashing and Obfuscation using Knuth's Algorithm.
*   [passlib (‚≠ê282)](https://github.com/hlandau/passlib) - Futureproof password hashing library.
*   [secure (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/unrolled/secure) - HTTP middleware for Go that facilitates some quick security wins.
*   [secureio (‚≠ê29)](https://github.com/xaionaro-go/secureio) - An keyexchanging+authenticating+encrypting wrapper and multiplexer for `io.ReadWriteCloser` based on XChaCha20-poly1305, ECDH and ED25519.
*   [simple-scrypt (‚≠ê184)](https://github.com/elithrar/simple-scrypt) - Scrypt package with a simple, obvious API and automatic cost calibration built-in.
*   [ssh-vault (‚≠ê378)](https://github.com/ssh-vault/ssh-vault) - encrypt/decrypt using ssh keys.
*   [sslmgr (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/adrianosela/sslmgr) - SSL certificates made easy with a high level wrapper around acme/autocert.
*   [themis (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) - high-level cryptographic library for solving typical data security tasks (secure data storage, secure messaging, zero-knowledge proof authentication), available for 14 languages, best fit for multi-platform apps.

### Serialization

*   [asn1 (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/PromonLogicalis/asn1) - Asn.1 BER and DER encoding library for golang.

*   [binstruct (‚≠ê69)](https://github.com/ghostiam/binstruct) - Golang binary decoder for mapping data into the structure.
*   [cbor (‚≠ê548)](https://github.com/fxamacker/cbor) - Small, safe, and easy CBOR encoding and decoding library.
*   [colfer (‚≠ê703)](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/colfer) - Code generation for the Colfer binary format.
*   [csvutil (‚≠ê794)](https://github.com/jszwec/csvutil) - High Performance, idiomatic CSV record encoding and decoding to native Go structures.
*   [elastic (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/epiclabs-io/elastic) - Convert slices, maps or any other unknown value across different types at run-time, no matter what.
*   [fixedwidth (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/huydang284/fixedwidth) - Fixed-width text formatting (UTF-8 supported).
*   [fwencoder (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) - Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go.
*   [go-capnproto (‚≠ê287)](https://github.com/glycerine/go-capnproto) - Cap'n Proto library and parser for go.
*   [go-codec (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/ugorji/go) - High Performance, feature-Rich, idiomatic encode, decode and rpc library for msgpack, cbor and json, with runtime-based OR code-generation support.
*   [go-lctree (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/sbourlon/go-lctree) - Provides a CLI and primitives to serialize and deserialize [LeetCode binary trees](https://support.leetcode.com/hc/en-us/articles/360011883654-What-does-1-null-2-3-mean-in-binary-tree-representation).
*   [gogoprotobuf (‚≠ê5.5k)](https://github.com/gogo/protobuf) - Protocol Buffers for Go with Gadgets.
*   [goprotobuf (‚≠ê9k)](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) - Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers.
*   [jsoniter (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) - High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json".
*   [mapstructure (‚≠ê6.8k)](https://github.com/mitchellh/mapstructure) - Go library for decoding generic map values into native Go structures.
*   [php\_session\_decoder (‚≠ê157)](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) - GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions.
*   [pletter (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) - A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers.
*   [structomap (‚≠ê139)](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) - Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures.
*   [unitpacking (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/recolude/unitpacking) - Library to pack unit vectors into as fewest bytes as possible.

### Server Applications

*   [algernon (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/xyproto/algernon) - HTTP/2 web server with built-in support for Lua, Markdown, GCSS and Amber.
*   [Caddy (‚≠ê47k)](https://github.com/caddyserver/caddy) - Caddy is an alternative, HTTP/2 web server that's easy to configure and use.
*   [consul](https://www.consul.io/) - Consul is a tool for service discovery, monitoring and configuration.
*   [cortex-tenant (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/cortex-tenant) - Prometheus remote write proxy that adds add Cortex tenant ID header based on metric labels.
*   [devd (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/cortesi/devd) - Local webserver for developers.
*   [discovery (‚≠ê1.7k)](https://github.com/Bilibili/discovery) - A registry for resilient mid-tier load balancing and failover.
*   [dudeldu (‚≠ê140)](https://github.com/krotik/dudeldu) - A simple SHOUTcast server.
*   [dummy (‚≠ê172)](https://github.com/neotoolkit/dummy) - Run mock server based off an API contract with one command.
*   [Easegress (‚≠ê5.1k)](https://github.com/megaease/easegress) - A cloud native high availability/performance traffic orchestration system with observability and extensibility.
*   [etcd (‚≠ê43k)](https://github.com/coreos/etcd) - Highly-available key value store for shared configuration and service discovery.
*   [Euterpe (‚≠ê465)](https://github.com/ironsmile/euterpe) - Self-hosted music streaming server with built-in web UI and REST API.
*   [Fider (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/getfider/fider) - Fider is an open platform to collect and organize customer feedback.
*   [Flagr (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/checkr/flagr) - Flagr is an open-source feature flagging and A/B testing service.
*   [flipt (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/markphelps/flipt) - A self contained feature flag solution written in Go and Vue.js
*   [go-feature-flag (‚≠ê677)](https://github.com/thomaspoignant/go-feature-flag) - A feature flag solution, with only a YAML file in the backend (S3, GitHub, HTTP, local file ...), no server to install, just add a file in a central system and refer to it.
*   [go-proxy-cache (‚≠ê89)](https://github.com/fabiocicerchia/go-proxy-cache) - Simple Reverse Proxy with Caching, written in Go, using Redis.
*   [jackal (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/ortuman/jackal) - An XMPP server written in Go.
*   [lets-proxy2 (‚≠ê75)](https://github.com/rekby/lets-proxy2) - Reverse proxy for handle https with issue certificates in fly from lets-encrypt.
*   [minio (‚≠ê38k)](https://github.com/minio/minio) - Minio is a distributed object storage server.
*   [Moxy (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/moxy) - Moxy is a simple mocker and proxy application server, you can create mock endpoints as well as proxy requests in case no mock exists for the endpoint.
*   [nginx-prometheus (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/nginx-prometheus) - Nginx log parser and exporter to Prometheus.
*   [nsq](https://nsq.io/) - A realtime distributed messaging platform.
*   [protoxy (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/camgraff/protoxy) - A proxy server that converts JSON request bodies to Protocol Buffers.
*   [psql-streamer (‚≠ê51)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/psql-streamer) - Stream database events from PostgreSQL to Kafka.
*   [riemann-relay (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/blind-oracle/riemann-relay) - Relay to load-balance Riemann events and/or convert them to Carbon.
*   [RoadRunner (‚≠ê7.1k)](https://github.com/spiral/roadrunner) - High-performance PHP application server, load-balancer and process manager.
*   [SFTPGo (‚≠ê5.9k)](https://github.com/drakkan/sftpgo) - Fully featured and highly configurable SFTP server with optional FTP/S and WebDAV support. It can serve local filesystem and Cloud Storage backends such as S3 and Google Cloud Storage.
*   [simple-jwt-provider (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/leberKleber/simple-jwt-provider) - Simple and lightweight provider which exhibits JWTs, supports login, password-reset (via mail) and user management.
*   [Trickster (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/tricksterproxy/trickster) - HTTP reverse proxy cache and time series accelerator.

### Stream Processing

*   [go-streams (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/reugn/go-streams) - Go stream processing library.
*   [machine (‚≠ê124)](https://github.com/whitaker-io/machine) - Go library for writing and generating stream workers with built in metrics and traceability.
*   [stream (‚≠ê77)](https://github.com/youthlin/stream) - Go Stream, like Java 8 Stream: Filter/Map/FlatMap/Peek/Sorted/ForEach/Reduce...

### Template Engines

*   [ego (‚≠ê553)](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) - Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled.
*   [extemplate (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/dannyvankooten/extemplate) - Tiny wrapper around html/template to allow for easy file-based template inheritance.
*   [fasttemplate (‚≠ê693)](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) - Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than [text/template](https://golang.org/pkg/text/template/).
*   [gospin (‚≠ê45)](https://github.com/m1/gospin) - Article spinning and spintax/spinning syntax engine, useful for A/B, testing pieces of text/articles and creating more natural conversations.
*   [goview (‚≠ê334)](https://github.com/foolin/goview) - Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application.
*   [jet (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/CloudyKit/jet) - Jet template engine.
*   [liquid (‚≠ê202)](https://github.com/osteele/liquid) - Go implementation of Shopify Liquid templates.
*   [maroto (‚≠ê982)](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) - A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple.
*   [pongo2 (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) - Django-like template-engine for Go.
*   [quicktemplate (‚≠ê2.7k)](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) - Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it.
*   [raymond (‚≠ê523)](https://github.com/aymerick/raymond) - Complete handlebars implementation in Go.
*   [Razor (‚≠ê812)](https://github.com/sipin/gorazor) - Razor view engine for Golang.
*   [Soy (‚≠ê169)](https://github.com/robfig/soy) - Closure templates (aka Soy templates) for Go, following the [official spec](https://developers.google.com/closure/templates/).
*   [sprig (‚≠ê3.5k)](https://github.com/Masterminds/sprig) - Useful template functions for Go templates.
*   [tbd (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/lucasepe/tbd) - A really simple way to create text templates with placeholders - exposes extra builtin Git repo metadata.

### Testing

*   Testing Frameworks

    *   [apitest](https://apitest.dev) - Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.
    *   [assert (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/go-playground/assert) - Basic Assertion Library used along side native go testing, with building blocks for custom assertions.
    *   [badio (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/cavaliercoder/badio) - Extensions to Go's `testing/iotest` package.
    *   [baloo (‚≠ê754)](https://github.com/h2non/baloo) - Expressive and versatile end-to-end HTTP API testing made easy.
    *   [be (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/be) - The minimalist generic test assertion library.
    *   [biff (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/fulldump/biff) - Bifurcation testing framework, BDD compatible.
    *   [charlatan (‚≠ê197)](https://github.com/percolate/charlatan) - Tool to generate fake interface implementations for tests.
    *   [commander (‚≠ê212)](https://github.com/SimonBaeumer/commander) - Tool for testing cli applications on windows, linux and osx.
    *   [covergates (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/covergates/covergates) - Self-hosted code coverage report review and management service.
    *   [cupaloy (‚≠ê261)](https://github.com/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy) - Simple snapshot testing addon for your test framework.
    *   [dbcleaner (‚≠ê151)](https://github.com/khaiql/dbcleaner) - Clean database for testing purpose, inspired by `database_cleaner` in Ruby.
    *   [dsunit (‚≠ê42)](https://github.com/viant/dsunit) - Datastore testing for SQL, NoSQL, structured files.
    *   [embedded-postgres (‚≠ê561)](https://github.com/fergusstrange/embedded-postgres) - Run a real Postgres database locally on Linux, OSX or Windows as part of another Go application or test.
    *   [endly (‚≠ê238)](https://github.com/viant/endly) - Declarative end to end functional testing.
    *   [fixenv (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/rekby/fixenv) - Fixture manage engine, inspired by pytest fixtures.
    *   [fluentassert (‚≠ê32)](https://github.com/fluentassert/verify) - Extensible, type-safe, fluent assertion Go library.
    *   [flute (‚≠ê17)](https://github.com/suzuki-shunsuke/flute) - HTTP client testing framework.
    *   [frisby (‚≠ê273)](https://github.com/verdverm/frisby) - REST API testing framework.
    *   [gherkingen (‚≠ê57)](https://github.com/hedhyw/gherkingen) - BDD boilerplate generator and framework.
    *   [ginkgo](https://onsi.github.io/ginkgo/) - BDD Testing Framework for Go.
    *   [gnomock (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/orlangure/gnomock) - integration testing with real dependencies (database, cache, even Kubernetes or AWS) running in Docker, without mocks.
    *   [go-carpet (‚≠ê236)](https://github.com/msoap/go-carpet) - Tool for viewing test coverage in terminal.
    *   [go-cmp (‚≠ê3.4k)](https://github.com/google/go-cmp) - Package for comparing Go values in tests.
    *   [go-hit (‚≠ê210)](https://github.com/Eun/go-hit) - Hit is an http integration test framework written in golang.
    *   [go-mutesting (‚≠ê581)](https://github.com/zimmski/go-mutesting) - Mutation testing for Go source code.
    *   [go-mysql-test-container (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/arikama/go-mysql-test-container) - Golang MySQL testcontainer to help with MySQL integration testing.
    *   [go-snaps (‚≠ê57)](http://github.com/gkampitakis/go-snaps) - Jest-like snapshot testing in Golang.
    *   [go-testdeep (‚≠ê374)](https://github.com/maxatome/go-testdeep) - Extremely flexible golang deep comparison, extends the go testing package.
    *   [go-testpredicate (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/maargenton/go-testpredicate) - Test predicate style assertions library with extensive diagnostics output.
    *   [go-vcr (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/dnaeon/go-vcr) - Record and replay your HTTP interactions for fast, deterministic and accurate tests.
    *   [goblin (‚≠ê882)](https://github.com/franela/goblin) - Mocha like testing framework fo Go.
    *   [goc (‚≠ê657)](https://github.com/qiniu/goc) - Goc is a comprehensive coverage testing system for The Go Programming Language.
    *   [gocheck](https://labix.org/gocheck) - More advanced testing framework alternative to gotest.
    *   [GoConvey (‚≠ê7.7k)](https://github.com/smartystreets/goconvey/) - BDD-style framework with web UI and live reload.
    *   [gocrest (‚≠ê94)](https://github.com/corbym/gocrest) - Composable hamcrest-like matchers for Go assertions.
    *   [godog (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/cucumber/godog) - Cucumber BDD framework for Go.
    *   [gofight (‚≠ê435)](https://github.com/appleboy/gofight) - API Handler Testing for Golang Router framework.
    *   [gogiven (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/corbym/gogiven) - YATSPEC-like BDD testing framework for Go.
    *   [gomatch (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/jfilipczyk/gomatch) - library created for testing JSON against patterns.
    *   [gomega](https://onsi.github.io/gomega/) - Rspec like matcher/assertion library.
    *   [Gont (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/stv0g/gont) - Go network testing toolkit for testing building complex network topologies using Linux namespaces.
    *   [GoSpec (‚≠ê113)](https://github.com/orfjackal/gospec) - BDD-style testing framework for the Go programming language.
    *   [gospecify (‚≠ê53)](https://github.com/stesla/gospecify) - This provides a BDD syntax for testing your Go code. It should be familiar to anybody who has used libraries such as rspec.
    *   [gosuite (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/pavlo/gosuite) - Brings lightweight test suites with setup/teardown facilities to `testing` by leveraging Go1.7's Subtests.
    *   [got (‚≠ê261)](https://github.com/ysmood/got) - An enjoyable golang test framework.
    *   [gotest.tools (‚≠ê416)](https://github.com/gotestyourself/gotest.tools) - A collection of packages to augment the go testing package and support common patterns.
    *   [Hamcrest (‚≠ê28)](https://github.com/rdrdr/hamcrest) - fluent framework for declarative Matcher objects that, when applied to input values, produce self-describing results.
    *   [httpexpect (‚≠ê2.2k)](https://github.com/gavv/httpexpect) - Concise, declarative, and easy to use end-to-end HTTP and REST API testing.
    *   [is (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/matryer/is) - Professional lightweight testing mini-framework for Go.
    *   [jsonassert (‚≠ê104)](https://github.com/kinbiko/jsonassert) - Package for verifying that your JSON payloads are serialized correctly.
    *   [omg.testingtools (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.testingtools) - The simple library for change a values of private fields for testing.
    *   [restit (‚≠ê56)](https://github.com/yookoala/restit) - Go micro framework to help writing RESTful API integration test.
    *   [schema (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/jgroeneveld/schema) - Quick and easy expression matching for JSON schemas used in requests and responses.
    *   [stop-and-go (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/elgohr/stop-and-go) - Testing helper for concurrency.
    *   [testcase (‚≠ê107)](https://github.com/adamluzsi/testcase) - Idiomatic testing framework for Behavior Driven Development.
    *   [testcontainers-go (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/testcontainers/testcontainers-go) - A Go package that makes it simple to create and clean up container-based dependencies for automated integration/smoke tests. The clean, easy-to-use API enables developers to programmatically define containers that should be run as part of a test and clean up those resources when the test is done.
    *   [testfixtures (‚≠ê918)](https://github.com/go-testfixtures/testfixtures) - A helper for Rails' like test fixtures to test database applications.
    *   [Testify (‚≠ê19k)](https://github.com/stretchr/testify) - Sacred extension to the standard go testing package.
    *   [testmd](https://godoc.org/github.com/tvastar/test/cmd/testmd) - Convert markdown snippets into testable go code.
    *   [testsql (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/zhulongcheng/testsql) - Generate test data from SQL files before testing and clear it after finished.
    *   [testza (‚≠ê409)](https://github.com/MarvinJWendt/testza) - Full-featured test framework with nice colorized output.
    *   [trial (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/jgroeneveld/trial) - Quick and easy extendable assertions without introducing much boilerplate.
    *   [Tt (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/vcaesar/tt) - Simple and colorful test tools.
    *   [wstest (‚≠ê99)](https://github.com/posener/wstest) - Websocket client for unit-testing a websocket http.Handler.
*   Mock

    *   [counterfeiter (‚≠ê797)](https://github.com/maxbrunsfeld/counterfeiter) - Tool for generating self-contained mock objects.
    *   [genmock](https://gitlab.com/so_literate/genmock) - Go mocking system with code generator for building calls of the interface methods.
    *   [go-localstack (‚≠ê64)](https://github.com/elgohr/go-localstack) - Tool for using localstack in AWS testing.
    *   [go-sqlmock (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/DATA-DOG/go-sqlmock) - Mock SQL driver for testing database interactions.
    *   [go-txdb (‚≠ê523)](https://github.com/DATA-DOG/go-txdb) - Single transaction based database driver mainly for testing purposes.
    *   [gock (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/h2non/gock) - Versatile HTTP mocking made easy.
    *   [gomock (‚≠ê8.7k)](https://github.com/golang/mock) - Mocking framework for the Go programming language.
    *   [govcr (‚≠ê145)](https://github.com/seborama/govcr) - HTTP mock for Golang: record and replay HTTP interactions for offline testing.
    *   [hoverfly (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/SpectoLabs/hoverfly) - HTTP(S) proxy for recording and simulating REST/SOAP APIs with extensible middleware and easy-to-use CLI.
    *   [httpmock (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/jarcoal/httpmock) - Easy mocking of HTTP responses from external resources.
    *   [minimock (‚≠ê493)](https://github.com/gojuno/minimock) - Mock generator for Go interfaces.
    *   [mockery (‚≠ê4.5k)](https://github.com/vektra/mockery) - Tool to generate Go interfaces.
    *   [mockhttp (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/tv42/mockhttp) - Mock object for Go http.ResponseWriter.
    *   [mockit (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/pasdam/mockit) - Allows functions and method easy mocking, without defining new types; it's similar to Mockito for Java.
    *   [mooncake (‚≠ê17)](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/mooncake) - A simple way to generate mocks for multiple purposes
    *   [timex (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/cabify/timex) - A test-friendly replacement for the native `time` package.
*   Fuzzing and delta-debugging/reducing/shrinking.

    *   [go-fuzz (‚≠ê4.6k)](https://github.com/dvyukov/go-fuzz) - Randomized testing system.
    *   [gofuzz (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/google/gofuzz) - Library for populating go objects with random values.
    *   [Tavor (‚≠ê243)](https://github.com/zimmski/tavor) - Generic fuzzing and delta-debugging framework.
*   Selenium and browser control tools.

    *   [cdp (‚≠ê673)](https://github.com/mafredri/cdp) - Type-safe bindings for the Chrome Debugging Protocol that can be used with browsers or other debug targets that implement it.
    *   [chromedp (‚≠ê8.9k)](https://github.com/knq/chromedp) - a way to drive/test Chrome, Safari, Edge, Android Webviews, and other browsers supporting the Chrome Debugging Protocol.
    *   [ggr (‚≠ê303)](https://github.com/aerokube/ggr) - a lightweight server that routes and proxies Selenium WebDriver requests to multiple Selenium hubs.
    *   [playwright-go (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/mxschmitt/playwright-go) - browser automation library to control Chromium, Firefox and WebKit with a single API.
    *   [rod (‚≠ê3.7k)](https://github.com/go-rod/rod) - A Devtools driver to make web automation and scraping easy.
    *   [selenoid (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/aerokube/selenoid) - alternative Selenium hub server that launches browsers within containers.
*   Fail injection
    *   [failpoint (‚≠ê770)](https://github.com/pingcap/failpoint) - An implementation of [failpoints](https://www.freebsd.org/cgi/man.cgi?query=fail) for Golang.

*   [slice (‚≠ê49)](https://github.com/psampaz/slice) - Type-safe functions for common Go slice operations.
*   [sliceconv (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/Henry-Sarabia/sliceconv) - Slice conversion between primitive types.
*   [slicer (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/leaanthony/slicer) - Makes working with slices easier.
*   [sorty (‚≠ê119)](https://github.com/jfcg/sorty) - Fast Concurrent / Parallel Sorting.
*   [sqlx (‚≠ê14k)](https://github.com/jmoiron/sqlx) - provides a set of extensions on top of the excellent built-in database/sql package.
*   [sshman (‚≠ê43)](https://github.com/shoobyban/sshman) - SSH Manager for authorized\_keys files on multiple remote servers.
*   [statiks (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/janiltonmaciel/statiks) - Fast, zero-configuration, static HTTP filer server.
*   [Storm (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/asdine/storm) - Simple and powerful toolkit for BoltDB.
*   [structs (‚≠ê21)](https://github.com/PumpkinSeed/structs) - Implement simple functions to manipulate structs.
*   [throttle (‚≠ê30)](https://github.com/yudppp/throttle) - Throttle is an object that will perform exactly one action per duration.
*   [tik (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/andy2046/tik) - Simple and easy timing wheel package for Go.
*   [tome (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/cyruzin/tome) - Tome was designed to paginate simple RESTful APIs.
*   [toolbox (‚≠ê191)](https://github.com/viant/toolbox) - Slice, map, multimap, struct, function, data conversion utilities. Service router, macro evaluator, tokenizer.
*   [ugo (‚≠ê27)](https://github.com/alxrm/ugo) - ugo is slice toolbox with concise syntax for Go.
*   [UNIS (‚≠ê70)](https://github.com/esemplastic/unis) - Common Architecture‚Ñ¢ for String Utilities in Go.
*   [usql (‚≠ê8k)](https://github.com/knq/usql) - usql is a universal command-line interface for SQL databases.
*   [util (‚≠ê274)](https://github.com/shomali11/util) - Collection of useful utility functions. (strings, concurrency, manipulations, ...).
*   [wuzz (‚≠ê10k)](https://github.com/asciimoo/wuzz) - Interactive cli tool for HTTP inspection.
*   [xferspdy (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/monmohan/xferspdy) - Xferspdy provides binary diff and patch library in golang.

### UUID

*   [goid (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) - Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs.
*   [gouid (‚≠ê19)](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) - Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation.
*   [nanoid (‚≠ê59)](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) - A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator.
*   [sno (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/muyo/sno) - Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata.
*   [ulid (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) - Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier).
*   [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq) - No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/agext/uuid) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) - Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid.
*   [uuid (‚≠ê4.3k)](https://github.com/google/uuid) - Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services.
*   [wuid (‚≠ê491)](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) - An extremely fast globally unique number generator.
*   [xid (‚≠ê3.3k)](https://github.com/rs/xid) - Xid is a globally unique id generator library, ready to be safely used directly in your server code.

### Validation

*   [checkdigit (‚≠ê98)](https://github.com/osamingo/checkdigit) - Provide check digit algorithms (Luhn, Verhoeff, Damm) and calculators (ISBN, EAN, JAN, UPC, etc.).

*   [jio (‚≠ê74)](https://github.com/faceair/jio) - jio is a json schema validator similar to [joi (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/hapijs/joi).
*   [ozzo-validation (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-validation) - Supports validation of various data types (structs, strings, maps, slices, etc.) with configurable and extensible validation rules specified in usual code constructs instead of struct tags.
*   [validate (‚≠ê869)](https://github.com/gookit/validate) - Go package for data validation and filtering. support validate Map, Struct, Request(Form, JSON, url.Values, Uploaded Files) data and more features.
*   [validate (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/gobuffalo/validate) - This package provides a framework for writing validations for Go applications.
*   [validator (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/go-playground/validator) - Go Struct and Field validation, including Cross Field, Cross Struct, Map, Slice and Array diving.

### Middlewares / Actual middlewares

*   [client-timing (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
*   [CORS (‚≠ê2.3k)](https://github.com/rs/cors) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
*   [formjson (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/rs/formjson) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
*   [go-fault (‚≠ê478)](https://github.com/github/go-fault) - Fault injection middleware for Go.
*   [go-server-timing (‚≠ê850)](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) - Add/parse Server-Timing header.
*   [Limiter (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
*   [ln-paywall (‚≠ê132)](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
*   [mid (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/bobg/mid) - Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more.
*   [rk-gin (‚≠ê41)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [rk-grpc (‚≠ê63)](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
*   [Tollbooth (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
*   [XFF (‚≠ê96)](https://github.com/sebest/xff) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

### Middlewares / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alice (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/justinas/alice) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
*   [catena (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
*   [chain (‚≠ê65)](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
*   [gores (‚≠ê100)](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
*   [interpose (‚≠ê295)](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
*   [mediary (‚≠ê82)](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) - add interceptors to `http.Client` to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
*   [muxchain (‚≠ê209)](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
*   [negroni (‚≠ê7.3k)](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
*   [render (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/unrolled/render) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
*   [renderer (‚≠ê255)](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) - Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go.
*   [rye (‚≠ê101)](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.
*   [stats (‚≠ê589)](https://github.com/thoas/stats) - Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.

### Routers / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [alien (‚≠ê127)](https://github.com/gernest/alien) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
*   [bellt (‚≠ê54)](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt) - A simple Go HTTP router.
*   [Bone (‚≠ê1.3k)](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) - Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
*   [Bxog (‚≠ê105)](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) - Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
*   [chi (‚≠ê14k)](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) - Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
*   [fasthttprouter (‚≠ê873)](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) - High performance router forked from `httprouter`. The first router fit for `fasthttp`.
*   [FastRouter (‚≠ê22)](https://github.com/razonyang/fastrouter) - a fast, flexible HTTP router written in Go.
*   [gocraft/web (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/gocraft/web) - Mux and middleware package in Go.
*   [Goji (‚≠ê938)](https://github.com/goji/goji) - Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for `net/context`.
*   [goroute (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/goroute/route) - Simple yet powerful HTTP request multiplexer.
*   [GoRouter (‚≠ê146)](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) - GoRouter is a Server/API micro framework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting `net/context`.
*   [gowww/router (‚≠ê165)](https://github.com/gowww/router) - Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
*   [httprouter (‚≠ê15k)](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
*   [httptreemux (‚≠ê586)](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
*   [lars (‚≠ê387)](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
*   [mux (‚≠ê18k)](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
*   [ngamux (‚≠ê56)](https://github.com/ngamux/ngamux) - Simple HTTP router for Go.
*   [ozzo-routing (‚≠ê447)](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
*   [pure (‚≠ê137)](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
*   [Siesta (‚≠ê351)](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) - Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
*   [vestigo (‚≠ê268)](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) - Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
*   [violetear (‚≠ê106)](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) - Go HTTP router.
*   [xmux (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/rs/xmux) - High performance muxer based on `httprouter` with `net/context` support.
*   [xujiajun/gorouter (‚≠ê532)](https://github.com/xujiajun/gorouter) - A simple and fast HTTP router for Go.

### XML / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

### Zero Trust / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [Cosign (‚≠ê3.2k)](https://github.com/sigstore/cosign) - Container Signing, Verification and Storage in an OCI registry.
*   [in-toto (‚≠ê83)](https://github.com/in-toto/in-toto-golang) - Go implementation of the in-toto (provides a framework to protect the integrity of the software supply chain) python reference implementation.
*   [Spiffe-Vault (‚≠ê56)](https://github.com/philips-labs/spiffe-vault) - Utilizes Spiffe JWT authentication with Hashicorp Vault for secretless authentication.
*   [Spire (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/spiffe/spire) - SPIRE (the SPIFFE Runtime Environment) is a toolchain of APIs for establishing trust between software systems across a wide variety of hosting platforms.

### Code Analysis / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [apicompat (‚≠ê177)](https://github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat) - Checks recent changes to a Go project for backwards incompatible changes.
*   [ChainJacking (‚≠ê38)](https://github.com/Checkmarx/chainjacking) - Find which of your Go lang direct GitHub dependencies is susceptible to ChainJacking attack.
*   [dupl (‚≠ê307)](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) - Tool for code clone detection.
*   [errcheck (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/kisielk/errcheck) - Errcheck is a program for checking for unchecked errors in Go programs.
*   [gcvis (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/davecheney/gcvis) - Visualise Go program GC trace data in real time.
*   [go-checkstyle (‚≠ê127)](https://github.com/qiniu/checkstyle) - checkstyle is a style check tool like java checkstyle. This tool inspired by java checkstyle, golint. The style referred to some points in Go Code Review Comments.
*   [go-cleanarch (‚≠ê715)](https://github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch) - go-cleanarch was created to validate Clean Architecture rules, like a The Dependency Rule and interaction between packages in your Go projects.
*   [go-critic (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/go-critic/go-critic) - source code linter that brings checks that are currently not implemented in other linters.
*   [go-mod-outdated (‚≠ê625)](https://github.com/psampaz/go-mod-outdated) - An easy way to find outdated dependencies of your Go projects.
*   [go-outdated (‚≠ê44)](https://github.com/firstrow/go-outdated) - Console application that displays outdated packages.
*   [goast-viewer (‚≠ê697)](https://github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer) - Web based Golang AST visualizer.
*   [goimports](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goimports) - Tool to fix (add, remove) your Go imports automatically.
*   [golang-ifood-sdk (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk) - iFood API SDK.
*   [golines (‚≠ê588)](https://github.com/segmentio/golines) - Formatter that automatically shortens long lines in Go code.
*   [GoLint (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/golang/lint) - Golint is a linter for Go source code.
*   [GoPlantUML (‚≠ê1.4k)](https://github.com/jfeliu007/goplantuml) - Library and CLI that generates text plantump class diagram containing information about structures and interfaces with the relationship among them.
*   [goreturns](https://sourcegraph.com/github.com/sqs/goreturns) - Adds zero-value return statements to match the func return types.
*   [gosimple (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/gosimple) - gosimple is a linter for Go source code that specialises on simplifying code.
*   [gostatus (‚≠ê244)](https://github.com/shurcooL/gostatus) - Command line tool, shows the status of repositories that contain Go packages.
*   [lint (‚≠ê67)](https://github.com/surullabs/lint) - Run linters as part of go test.
*   [php-parser (‚≠ê912)](https://github.com/z7zmey/php-parser) - A Parser for PHP written in Go.
*   [staticcheck (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck) - staticcheck is `go vet` on steroids, applying a ton of static analysis checks you might be used to from tools like ReSharper for C#.
*   [tickgit (‚≠ê304)](https://github.com/augmentable-dev/tickgit) - CLI and go package for surfacing code comment TODOs (in any language) and applying a `git blame`to identify the author.
*   [todocheck (‚≠ê394)](https://github.com/preslavmihaylov/todocheck) - Static code analyser which links TODO comments in code with issues in your issue tracker.
*   [unconvert (‚≠ê348)](https://github.com/mdempsky/unconvert) - Remove unnecessary type conversions from Go source.
*   [unused (‚≠ê5.3k)](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/unused) - unused checks Go code for unused constants, variables, functions and types.
*   [validate (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/mccoyst/validate) - Automatically validates struct fields with tags.

*   [mockingjay (‚≠ê535)](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) - Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests.
*   [myLG (‚≠ê2.6k)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) - Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go.
*   [naclpipe (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) - Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go.
*   [Neo-cowsay (‚≠ê245)](https://github.com/Code-Hex/Neo-cowsay) - üêÆ cowsay is reborn. for a New Era.
*   [nes (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) emulator written in Go.
*   [Orbit (‚≠ê175)](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) - A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates.
*   [peg (‚≠ê907)](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) - Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator.
*   [Plik (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/root-gg/plik) - Plik is a temporary file upload system (Wetransfer like) in Go.
*   [protoncheck (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/servusdei2018/protoncheck) - ProtonMail module for waybar/polybar/yabar/i3blocks.
*   [restic (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/restic/restic) - De-duplicating backup program.
*   [scc (‚≠ê4.6k)](https://github.com/boyter/scc) - Sloc Cloc and Code, a very fast accurate code counter with complexity calculations and COCOMO estimates.
*   [Seaweed File System (‚≠ê17k)](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) disk seek.
*   [shell2http (‚≠ê1.1k)](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control).
*   [snap (‚≠ê1.8k)](https://github.com/intelsdi-x/snap) - Powerful telemetry framework.
*   [Snitch (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/lucasgomide/snitch) - Simple way to notify your team and many tools when someone has deployed any application via Tsuru.
*   [Stack Up (‚≠ê2.4k)](https://github.com/pressly/sup) - Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers.
*   [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/) - Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
*   [tcpdog (‚≠ê223)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpdog) - eBPF based TCP observability.
*   [tcpprobe (‚≠ê335)](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpprobe) - TCP tool for network performance and path monitoring, including socket statistics.
*   [term-quiz (‚≠ê23)](https://github.com/crazcalm/term-quiz) - Quizzes for your terminal.
*   [toxiproxy (‚≠ê9k)](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) - Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests.
*   [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/) - Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
*   [vaku (‚≠ê146)](https://github.com/lingrino/vaku) - CLI & API for folder-based functions in Vault like copy, move, and search.
*   [vFlow (‚≠ê977)](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) - High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector.
*   [wellington (‚≠ê302)](https://github.com/wellington/wellington) - Sass project management tool, extends the language with sprite functions (like Compass).
*   [woke (‚≠ê369)](https://github.com/get-woke/woke) - Detect non-inclusive language in your source code.

### Benchmarks / Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

*   [autobench (‚≠ê96)](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
*   [go-benchmark-app (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with –êb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.

*   [go-web-framework-benchmark (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) - Go web framework benchmark.

*   [golang-sql-benchmark (‚≠ê64)](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
*   [gospeed (‚≠ê111)](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
*   [kvbench (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark.
*   [skynet (‚≠ê1k)](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
*   [speedtest-resize (‚≠ê231)](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) - Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language.
